<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">Indicate by check mark whether the
registrant is an emerging growth company as defined in Rule&#160;405 of the Securities Act of 1933 or Rule&#160;12b-2 of the Securities
Exchange Act of 1934. Emerging growth company <span id="xdx_902_edei--EntityEmergingGrowthCompany_c20231107__20231107_zSoOB9KCPqu" style="font-family: Wingdings"><ix:nonNumeric contextRef="AsOf2023-11-07" format="ixt:booleantrue" name="dei:EntityEmergingGrowthCompany">&#120;</ix:nonNumeric></span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">If an emerging growth company, indicate by check mark if the registrant
has elected not to use the extended transition period for complying with any new or revised financial accounting standards provided pursuant
to Section 13(a) of the Exchange Act. <span style="font-family: Wingdings"><span id="xdx_906_edei--EntityExTransitionPeriod_c20231107__20231107_zv8KSuCMNX1h"><ix:nonNumeric contextRef="AsOf2023-11-07" format="ixt:booleanfalse" name="dei:EntityExTransitionPeriod">&#168;</ix:nonNumeric></span></span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><b>Item 2.02 Results of Operations and Financial
Condition.</b></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in">On November 7, 2023, Runway
Growth Finance Corp. (the &#8220;Company&#8221;) issued a press release announcing its financial results for the quarter ended September
30, 2023. The text of the press release is included as Exhibit 99.1 to this Current Report on Form 8-K and is incorporated herein by reference.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in">The information set forth
under this Item 2.02, including the information set forth in Exhibit 99.1 hereto, is being &#8220;furnished&#8221; and shall not be deemed
&#8220;filed&#8221; for purposes of Section 18 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended (the &#8220;Exchange Act&#8221;), or
otherwise. The information set forth under this Item 2.02, including Exhibit 99.1, shall not be incorporated by reference into any registration
statement or other document pursuant to the Securities Act of 1933, as amended, or into any filing or other document pursuant to the Exchange
Act, except as otherwise expressly stated in any such filing.</p>

<P STYLE="margin: 0; text-align: right"><B>Exhibit 99.1</B></P>

<P STYLE="margin: 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="margin: 0; text-align: right"><IMG SRC="image_001.jpg" ALT=""></P>

<P STYLE="margin: 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 14pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center"><B>Runway Growth Finance Corp.
Reports Third Quarter 2023 Financial Results</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center">Delivered Total and Net Investment
Income of $43.8 and $22.0 Million, Respectively</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center">Investment Portfolio of $1.0 Billion</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center">Conference Call Today, Tuesday,
November 7, at 5:00 p.m. ET</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">MENLO PARK, Calif., November 7, 2023&mdash;Runway Growth Finance Corp.
(Nasdaq: RWAY) (&ldquo;Runway Growth&rdquo; or the &ldquo;Company&rdquo;), a leading provider of flexible capital solutions to late-
and growth-stage companies seeking an alternative to raising equity, today announced its financial results for the third quarter ended
September 30, 2023.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><B>Third Quarter 2023 Highlights</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="width: 100%; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Symbol">&middot;</FONT></TD><TD>Total investment income
                                            of $43.8 million</TD></TR></TABLE>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="width: 100%; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Symbol">&middot;</FONT></TD><TD>Net investment income
                                            of $22.0 million, or $0.54 per share</TD></TR></TABLE>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="width: 100%; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Symbol">&middot;</FONT></TD><TD>Net asset value of
                                            $14.08 per share</TD></TR></TABLE>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="width: 100%; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Symbol">&middot;</FONT></TD><TD>Dollar-weighted annualized
                                            yield on debt investments of 18.3% for the quarter</TD></TR></TABLE>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="width: 100%; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Symbol">&middot;</FONT></TD><TD>Six investments completed
                                            in new and existing portfolio companies, representing $40.8 million in funded loans</TD></TR></TABLE>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="width: 100%; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Symbol">&middot;</FONT></TD><TD>Aggregate proceeds
                                            of $125.3 million received from principal repayments</TD></TR></TABLE>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="width: 100%; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Symbol">&middot;</FONT></TD><TD>Declared fourth quarter
                                            2023 regular dividend of $0.40 per share</TD></TR></TABLE>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="width: 100%; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Symbol">&middot;</FONT></TD><TD>Declared fourth quarter
                                            2023 supplemental dividend of $0.06 per share</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&ldquo;Runway Growth&rsquo;s third quarter demonstrates
the resilience of our high quality, late-stage portfolio purpose-built to deliver superior credit performance,&rdquo; said Greg Greifeld,
Acting Chief Executive Officer of Runway Growth, and Deputy Chief Investment Officer and Head of Credit of Runway Growth Capital. &ldquo;Runway&rsquo;s
pipeline remains healthy and demand from companies for creative financing solutions is accelerating. Our team&rsquo;s evaluation standards
have never been higher as we seek to underwrite the right deals for Runway&rsquo;s stable and consistent portfolio.&rdquo;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">Greifeld continued, &ldquo;Runway
Growth&rsquo;s priority is preserving credit quality as we aim to protect our shareholders&rsquo; capital while generating attractive
returns. With industry low leverage and ample dry powder waiting to be deployed into a capital starved market, Runway is well positioned
to drive non-dilutive portfolio growth and ROE for shareholders as we approach 2024.&rdquo;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><B>Third Quarter 2023 Operating Results</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">Total investment income for the quarter ended September
30, 2023 was $43.8 million, compared to $27.0 million for the quarter ended September 30, 2022.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">Net investment income for the quarter ended September
30, 2023 was $22.0 million, or $0.54 per share, compared to $14.5 million, or $0.36 per share, for the quarter ended September 30, 2022.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">The Company's dollar-weighted annualized yield on
average debt investments for the quarter ended September 30, 2023 was 18.3%. The Company calculates the yield on dollar-weighted debt
investments for any period measured as (1) total investment-related income during the period divided by (2) the daily average of the
fair value of debt investments outstanding during the period.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"></P>

<!-- Field: Page; Sequence: 1 -->
    <DIV STYLE="margin-top: 12pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid"><P STYLE="margin: 0pt">&nbsp;</P></DIV>
    <DIV STYLE="break-before: page; margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 12pt"><P STYLE="margin: 0pt">&nbsp;</P></DIV>
    <!-- Field: /Page -->

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: right; margin: 0pt 0"><IMG SRC="image_001.jpg" ALT=""></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">Total operating expenses for the quarter ended September
30, 2023 were $21.7 million, compared to $12.5 million for the quarter ended September 30, 2022. The increase was driven by growing management
fees, incentive fees and interest expenses related to a larger loan portfolio and an increase in total borrowings at higher interest
rates.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">Net realized gain on investments was zero for the
quarter ended September 30, 2023, compared to a net realized gain of $0.4 million for the quarter ended September 30, 2022. The Company
experienced no credit losses during the third quarter or year-to-date in 2023.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">For the quarter ended September 30, 2023, net change
in unrealized loss on investments was $7.2 million, compared to a net change in unrealized loss of $3.2 million for the comparable prior
year period.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><B>Portfolio and Investment Activity</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">As of September 30, 2023, Runway Growth&rsquo;s investment
portfolio had an aggregate fair value of approximately $1,011 million and was comprised of approximately $962 million in term loans,
99% of which are senior secured loans and $49 million in warrants and other equity-related investments in 50 portfolio companies.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">During the third quarter of 2023, Runway Growth completed
six investments in new and existing portfolio companies, representing $40.8 million in funded loans.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">Total portfolio investment activity for the three
and nine months ended September 30, 2023, and 2022 was as follows:</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="border-collapse: collapse; width: 100%; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">

<P STYLE="margin: 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><B>Net Asset Value</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">As of September 30, 2023, net asset value (&ldquo;NAV&rsquo;&rdquo;)
per share was $14.08, compared to $14.12 as of September 30, 2022. Total net assets at the end of the third quarter of 2023 was $570.5
million, down 0.55% from $573.7 million in the prior year period.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">For the quarter ended September 30, 2023, net increase
in net assets resulting from operations was&nbsp;$14.8 million, or&nbsp;$0.37 per share, compared to a net increase in net assets of&nbsp;$11.7
million, or&nbsp;$0.29 per share, for the quarter ended&nbsp;September 30, 2022.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><B>Liquidity and Capital Resources</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">As of September 30, 2023, the Company had approximately
$311.9 million in available liquidity, including unrestricted cash and cash equivalents and $297.0 million in available borrowing capacity
under the Company&rsquo;s credit facility, subject to existing terms, advance rates and regulatory and covenant requirements.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">The Company ended the quarter with a core leverage
ratio of approximately 79%, compared to 97% for the quarter ended June 30, 2023.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><B>Distributions</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">On November 2, 2023, the Company&rsquo;s board of
directors declared a regular quarterly distribution of $0.40 per share for the fourth quarter of 2023, payable on November 28, 2023,
to stockholders of record as of November 13, 2023. In addition, the Company&rsquo;s board of directors declared a supplemental dividend
of $0.06 per share for the fourth quarter of 2023 that is also payable on November 28, 2023 to stockholders of record as of November
13, 2023.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><B>Share Repurchase Program</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">On November 2, 2023, the Company&rsquo;s board of
directors approved a share repurchase program (the &ldquo;Share Repurchase Program&rdquo;) under which the Company may repurchase up
to $25.0 million of its outstanding common stock. Under the Share Repurchase Program, purchases may be made at management&rsquo;s discretion
from time to time in open-market transactions, in accordance with all applicable securities laws and regulations.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><B>About Runway Growth Finance Corp.</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">Runway Growth is a growing specialty finance company focused on providing
flexible capital solutions to late- and growth-stage companies seeking an alternative to raising equity. Runway Growth is a closed-end
investment fund that has elected to be regulated as a business development company under the Investment Company Act of 1940. Runway Growth
is externally managed by Runway Growth Capital LLC, an established registered investment advisor that was formed in 2015 and led by industry
veteran David Spreng. For more information, please visit <U>www.runwaygrowth.com</U>.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

statement made herein. All forward-looking statements speak only as of the date of this press release.</P>

discussed herein. Please see a more detailed discussion of these risk factors and other related risks in the Company&rsquo;s most recent
annual Form 10-K report in the section entitled &ldquo;Risk Factors&rdquo;, which may be obtained on the Company&rsquo;s website www.runwaygrowth.com
or the SEC&rsquo;s website www.sec.gov.</P>
